itemProp="answer" itemType="http://schema.org/Answer" itemscope=""><h2 class="ContentItem-title"><div itemProp="zhihu:question" itemType="http://schema.org/Question" itemscope=""><meta itemProp="url" content="https://www.zhihu.com/question/312709782"/><meta itemProp="name" content="成为研究生后你都明白了什么?"/><a target="_blank" data-za-detail-view-element_name="Title" data-za-detail-view-id="2812" href="//www.zhihu.com/question/312709782/answer/1675427859">成为研究生后你都明白了什么?</a></div></h2><meta itemProp="image" content=""/><meta itemProp="upvoteCount" content="502"/><meta itemProp="url" content="https://www.zhihu.com/question/312709782/answer/1675427859"/><meta itemProp="dateCreated" content="2021-01-13T03:28:47.000Z"/><meta itemProp="dateModified" content="2021-01-20T08:10:13.000Z"/><meta itemProp="commentCount" content="31"/><div class="RichContent is-collapsed"><div class="RichContent-inner"><span class="RichText ztext 题，又不好意思打断你的汇报（但是可能引起导师的打断并吧啦吧啦一大段），而页码则是好做提问的定位。\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E分享\u002F讲述他人的文献一定记得标上作者和论文来源（给观\u002F听众选择的机会——顶级期刊或有意思的论文才有人会想听）。\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E8、有机会多去参加学术会议吧。\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E在会之时，可以听取相同领域的学者近期在研究什么、与其进行交流并学习；在会之外，是光明正大的旅游机会。\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E9、如果之前恋爱没有延续过来的，在研究生阶段谈一次恋爱不过分。\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E读博之时更难找对象，毕竟那是比996更享受赐福的一种福报状态；若是不继续读博，社会上谈恋爱和相亲则更现实一些。所以，请抓住即将一闪而逝的尾巴。\u003C\u002Fp\u003E","markInfos":[],"relationship":{"isThanked":false,"isNothelp":false,"voting":0,"upvotedFolloweeIds":[]},"isLabeled":false,"visitedCount":91861},"1710092035":{"id":1710092035,"type":"answer","url":"https:\u002F\u002Fapi.zhihu.com\u002Fanswers\u002F1710092035","author":{"id":"0","type":"people","url":"","userType":"people","urlToken":"","name":"匿名用户","headline":"","avatarUrl":"https:\u002F\u002Fpic4.zhimg.com\u002Faadd7b895_m.jpg"},"createdTime":1612192482,"updatedTime":1612361623,"voteupCount":2587,"thanksCount":164,"commentCount":188,"isCopyable":true,"question":{"id":48043247,"type":"question","url":"https:\u002F\u002Fapi.zhihu.com\u002Fquestions\u002F48043247","author":{"id":"c57cf5563468a78bf4a7d3a639365795","type":"people","url":"https:\u002F\u002Fapi.zhihu.com\u002Fpeople\u002Fc57cf5563468a78bf4a7d3a639365795","userType":"people","urlToken":"liu-min-62-80-11","name":"尾宿","headline":"你所看到的都是别人想让你看到的!","avatarUrl":"https:\u002F\u002Fpic3.zhimg.com\u002F50\u002Fv2-b644065fe20b6d8d17eae7e4ac04ab85_m.jpg","isOrg":false,"gender":1,"badge":[],"followersCount":135,"isFollowing":false,"isFollowed":false},"title":"你在父母面前遇到最尴尬的经历是怎样的？","created":1467354714,"answerCount":151,"followerCount":327,"commentCount":2,"boundTopicIds":[307,1309,7514,12262,13095],"isFollowing":false,"excerpt":"","relationship":{"isAuthor":false},"detail":"","questionType":"normal"},"thumbnail":"","excerpt":"就刚刚！！！我踏马！！ 汇报主题，又不好意思打断你的汇报（但是可能引起导师的打断并吧啦吧啦一大段），而页码则是好做提问的定位。\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E分享\u002F讲述他人的文献一定记得标上作者和论文来源（给观\u002F听众选择的机会——顶级期刊或有意思的论文才有人会想听）。\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E8、有机会多去参加学术会议吧。\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E在会之时，可以听取相同领域的学者近期在研究什么、与其进行交流并学习；在会之外，是光明正大的旅游机会。\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E9、如果之前恋爱没有延续过来的，在研究生阶段谈一次恋爱不过分。\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E读博之时更难找对象，毕竟那是比996更享受赐福的一种福报状态；若是不继续读博，社会上谈恋爱和相亲则更现实一些。所以，请抓住即将一闪而逝的尾巴。\u003C\u002Fp\u003E","mark_infos":[],"relationship":{"is_thanked":false,"is_nothelp":false,"voting":0,"upvoted_followee_ids":[]},"is_labeled":false,"visited_count":91861},"brief":"{\"source\":
